window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="Errors, MemberCenter_ProfileData, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since Aug 2008</p>
              <p>Lives in Bolingbrook, Illinois</p>
              <p> 50-64 year old male </p>
              <p>I love the three parts of travel: The planning, the going and the remembering. When I plan, I like to go deep and explore all the options, maximizing every opportunity. When I go, I like to be flexible using the plan as my starting place. When I remember, I like to write long, detailed Trip Reports and sort, edit and arrange my photos. First visits to places tend to be kind of manic, seeing and doing everything possible. When I find a place I love and then return to, I tend to be more relaxed. </p>
             </div>
            </div>
